 train kii lite sidhi jaati he or log trek par the

 aisi sthiti main train ko puri tarah rukne ke liye 700 meter kii aavashyaktaa hoti he
 Question-2: Was the train stopped after the accident? Officer: After reducing the speed of the train, the speed was increased to 7-10 kmph
 lekin guard ne kaha ki log patharav kar rahe hai

 train ko ghatnasthal par rokna thik nahin tha
 Question-3: Did the Railways have any information about the event? Officer: We had no information nor did anyone tell us that people will stay on the track
 hamaare paas yah bhi jaankaree nahin thi ki train ko dhimaa karnaa he
